<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 12.&#160;
Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On June 29, 2004, the Registrant issued a press release and held a
conference call with analysts to report on the results of operations for the
second quarter of fiscal year 2004, which ended on May 31, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furnished with this Form 8-K as Exhibit 99.1 is a copy
of the press release labeled &#147;McCormick Announces Record Second Quarter
Results,&#148; which includes an unaudited Consolidated Income Statement for the
three and six month periods ended May 31, 2004, an unaudited Consolidated
Balance Sheet of the Registrant as of May 31, 2004, and an unaudited
consolidated Statement of Cash Flows for the six months ended May 31, 2004.</font></p>

<DOCUMENT>

<SEQUENCE>2
<FILENAME>a04-7401_1ex99d1.htm
<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.1
<TEXT>
<html>

<head>



</head>

<body link="blue" vlink="purple">

<div style="font-family:'Times New Roman';">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:right;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK ANNOUNCES RECORD SECOND QUARTER RESULTS</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SPARKS, MD, JUNE 29 - - -
McCormick &amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), today reported record sales,
net income and earnings per share for the second quarter ended May 31, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales for the quarter
were $596 million, an increase of 13% versus the second quarter of 2003.&#160; Higher volume, pricing and product mix
contributed 9% of the increase of which 5% was attributable to the 2003
acquisition of Zatarain&#146;s.&#160; An increase
of 4% was added by favorable foreign exchange rates.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings per share from
continuing operations for the second quarter increased 11% to 30&#162; compared to
27&#162; in the second quarter of 2003.&#160; When
comparing the two quarters, the 3</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162; increase was the net result
of the following:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">An excellent performance from the Company&#146;s consumer and industrial
businesses contributed an increase of 5</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162; in the second quarter of
2004 compared to the prior year. </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;This was the
net result of higher sales, improved gross profit margin and a $4 million
increase in advertising expense.&#160; Gross
profit margin rose to 38.9% from 37.5% due to a positive shift in sales mix and
success with cost reduction initiatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the second quarter of 2004, the Company recorded income of $9 million
as a special credit related to the settlement of a class action lawsuit against
suppliers of flavor enhancers, increasing earnings per share by 4</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.&#160;
The Company will use these funds for various sales growth and cost
reduction initiatives throughout 2004.&#160;
In this regard, the Company recorded 2</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> of selling, general and administrative
expense in connection with a plan to reorganize administrative and other
functions in international locations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">These increases in earnings per share were further offset by a 1</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162; increase in
special charges</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> as
compared to the second quarter of 2003.&#160;
These charges related to the streamlining actions announced in early
2002.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Also, as compared to the second quarter of 2003, interest income for
the second quarter of 2004 was 3</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> less than in 2003, which was the period
during which the Company recorded a one-time interest payment in connection
with the final settlement of the purchase price for the Ducros acquisition</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In summary, the 3</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increase in earnings per share for the
second quarter of 2004 was the net result of a 5</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increase in operating results, a 4</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162; increase
from the lawsuit settlement, a 2&#162; decrease from reorganization expense, a 1&#162;
decrease</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> from special
charges and a 3</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#162;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> decrease in interest income related to the 2003 purchase price
settlement.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></p>


<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; For
the second quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer business rose 20% when
compared to 2003.&#160; Zatarain&#146;s added 11%
to sales, favorable foreign exchange added 5% and higher volume was the primary
driver of an additional 4%.&#160; Consumer
sales in the Americas rose 24% with 17% from the Zatarain&#146;s acquisition, 6%
primarily from higher volumes and 1% from foreign exchange.&#160; Sales volumes in the U.S. benefited from new
distribution gained in 2003 with a leading dollar store chain and a major
grocery retailer.&#160; In addition to these
volume increases, pricing was higher in the Americas for vanilla products in
response to higher vanilla bean costs<i><font style="font-style:italic;">.&#160; </font></i>Consumer sales in Europe
increased 13% for the quarter, with 12% due to favorable foreign exchange.&#160;&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region, sales increased
15% with 13% due to favorable foreign exchange and 2% due primarily to higher
volumes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Operating income from
continuing operations for the consumer business increased 25% to $46 million
for the second quarter of 2004.&#160; This
increase was driven by strong sales performance and increased margins, offset
in part by a $4 million increase in advertising related to new product
launches.&#160; Also affecting operating
income in the second quarter were costs of $3 million associated with the
reorganization of administrative and other functions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

Business</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the second quarter of
2004, sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business increased 7% when compared to
2003. Price and product mix were the primary drivers of a 4% increase, and
favorable foreign exchange added another 3%.&#160;
Higher costs for certain raw materials including vanilla, cheese and soy
oil led to higher prices.&#160; Continued
emphasis on more value-added products continues to improve the product mix for
this business.&#160; In the Americas,
industrial sales rose 5% with a continuation of strong sales to restaurant
customers driven in part by new products.&#160;
Industrial sales in Europe increased 13% for the quarter, with foreign
exchange contributing 14%. A shift in emphasis to higher margin food service
products resulted in reduced sales of certain lower margin products. In the
Asia/Pacific region, industrial sales rose 12%, with an 8% increase from foreign
exchange and the remaining increase from higher volumes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the second quarter of
2004, industrial business operating income declined 2% to $29 million.&#160;&#160; Higher sales and improved margins for the
quarter led to an increase of $3 million or 13% for this business.&#160; This was offset by a decrease of $4 million
in operating income due to costs associated with the reorganization of
administrative and other functions and special charges related to streamlining
actions announced early in 2002.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>


<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
</font>

<p align="center" style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Chairman&#146;s Comments</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Robert J. Lawless,
Chairman, President &amp; CEO, commented, &#147;We are pleased to report record
sales, net income and earnings per share for the second quarter and first half
of 2004.&#160; Employees throughout McCormick
are working to grow sales and improve efficiency, and we are seeing the results
of these efforts.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;As we assess our
progress mid-year in 2004, we have made great strides in four key areas:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;First, we have achieved impressive base business results
year-to-date.&#160; Net sales are up 15% with
5% from acquisitions, 5% from favorable foreign exchange and 5% from our core
businesses.&#160; This core business increase
is being driven by new products, new distribution, more effective marketing,
pricing and a continued shift to more value-added products.&#160; Success with our sales growth initiatives,
together with more efficient operations, added nearly a full percentage point
to gross profit margin.&#160; Cash from
operations was $66 million, up from $13 million in the first half of 2003.&#160; Our business has great momentum as we move
into the second half of 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Second, we have completed the transition of our U.S. industrial
businesses to the B2K program.&#160; This
means both consumer and industrial facilities in the U.S. are using a common
system and similar processes, positioning us to improve efficiency in all parts
of our operations.&#160; With these
capabilities and progress with supply chain initiatives, we are on track to
achieve our $15 million target of cost savings in 2004.&#160; The opportunity for future savings expands
as we move international operations onto the SAP platform in 2005.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Third, the integration plans for our 2003 acquisitions are on track,
and the sales and profit results from these businesses have exceeded our
expectations.&#160; We continue to seek
acquisitions that expand our flavor delivery for both the consumer and
industrial businesses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;And fourth, we received a settlement related to a class action lawsuit
in March 2004 and recorded income of $9 million in the second quarter.&#160; We have already begun to reinvest these
funds to grow sales and improve operations.&#160;
To that end, we have initiated a plan to reorganize administrative and
other functions in international locations.&#160;
We recorded costs of $4 million associated with this action in the
second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Given our first half
results and current financial projections, we expect sales for the year to
increase at a low double-digit rate.&#160;
Our earnings per share objective for 2004 remains in a $1.51 to $1.54
range as we invest in initiatives to grow sales and reduce costs.&#160;&#160; We continue to expect cash from operations
after net capital expenditures and dividends to exceed $100 million and have
been using a portion of this cash to repurchase shares.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We have reported great
results for the first half of 2004 and are excited about our new products,
marketing plans and cost improvements for the second half.&#160; We are highly confident that 2004 will be
another record year for McCormick. &#147;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p>
